in a protected corner but guide redeemer and benefactor advance on chaos and on the dark i pray god to give to you people the sentiment of the truth you have teach you people fond of its prosperity love peace well who would not love peace but allow I again sir to repeat with all possible emphasis the great word you speak nothing can bring you peace but the triumph of principle \* \* \* \* \* xlvi -- condition of europe -lrb- _ last speech in boston _ -rrb- on may 14th kossuth in obedience to a distinct invitation deliver in faneuil hall the follow ample speech or lecture on the present condition of europe lady and gentleman -- the gigantic struggle of the first french revolution associate the name of france so much with the cause of freedom in europe that all the world get accustom to see it take the lead in the struggle for european liberty and to look to it as a power entrust by providence with the initiation of revolution as a power without the impulse of which no liberal movement have any hope on the european continent i from my earliest day never share that opinion i feel always more sympathy with the anglo-saxon character and anglo-saxon institution which raise england notwithstanding its monarchy and its aristocracy to a position prouder than rome ever hold in its most glorious day : and which free from monarchical and aristocratical element here in america lie at the foundation of a political organization upon which the first true democratic republic be consolidated and develop into freedom power and prosperity in such a short time as to make it a live wonder to the contemporary age and a book full of instruction to the come generation however that opinion about the french initiative prevail in europe and it be a great misfortune for you know that france have always as yet forsake the movement which it raise in europe and the other nation act not spontaneously but only follow the impulse which the french have impart to they falter and stop at once as soon as the french fail they with that opinion of the french supremacy no revolution in europe could have a definite happy issue freedom never yet be give to nation as a gift but only as a reward bravely earn by one 's own exertion own sacrifice and own toil and never will never shall it be attain otherwise i speak therefore out of profound conviction when i say that though the heart of the philanthropist must feel pained at the new hard trial to which the french nation be and will yet be expose by the momentary success of loui napoleon bonaparte 's inglorious usurpation still that very fact will prove advantageous to the ultimate success of liberty in europe loui napoleon 's _ coup d'état _ much against he will have emancipate europe from its reliance upon france the combined initiative of nation have succeed to the initiative of france spontaneity and self-reliance have replace the depend on foreign impulse and reliance upon foreign aid france be reduce to the level amongst nation oblige to join general combination instead of regulate they and this i take for a very great advantage many have wonder at the momentary success of loui napoleon and be incline to take it for a evidence that the french nation be either not capable or not worthy to be free but that be a great fallacy the momentary success of loui napoleon be rather a evidence that france be _ thoroughly democratic _ all the revolution in france have result in the preponderance of that class which bear the denomination of _ bourgeoisie _ amongst all possible modification of oppression none be more detest by the people than oppression by a assembly the national assembly of france be the most treacherous the world have ever yet know issue from universal suffrage it go so far as to abolish universal suffrage and every day of its existence be a new blow stricken at democracy for the profit of the bourgeoisie loui napoleon have beat asunder that assembly which the french democracy have so many reason to hate and to despise and the people applaud he as the people of england applaud cromwell when he whip out the rump parliament but by what means be loui napoleon permit to do even what the people like to see do by no other means but by flattering the principle of democracy he restore the universal suffrage it be a execrable trick to be sure -- it be a shadow give for reality but still it prove that the democratic spirit be so consolidated in france that even despotic ambition must flatter it well depend upon it this democracy which the victorious usurper feel himself constrain to flatter in the brightest moment of he triumph -- this democracy will either make out of loui napoleon _ a tool _ which in spite of itself serve the democracy or it will crush he france be the country of sudden change and of unthought of accident i therefore will not presume to tell the event of its next week but one alternative i dare to state : loui napoleon either fall or maintain himself the fall of loui napoleon even if bring about by the old monarchical party can have no other issue than a republic -- a republic more faithful to the community of freedom in europe than all the former revolution have be or if loui napoleon maintain himself he can do so only either by rely upon the army or by flattering the feeling and interest of the mass if he rely upon the army he must give to it glory and profit or in other word he must give to it war well a war of france against whomsoever it be or for whatever purpose be the best possible chance for the success of a european revolution or if loui napoleon rely upon the feeling of the mass -- as indeed he appear willing to do -- in that case in spite of himself he become a tool in the hand of democracy and if by become such he forsake the allegiance of he master -- the league of absolutistical power -- well he will either be force to attack they or be attack by they so much for france now as to italy italy the sunny garden of europe whose blossom be blighted by the icy north wind from st petersburg -- italy that capture nightingale place under a fragrant bush of rose beneath a ever blue sky italy be always the battlefield of the contend principle since hundred of year ago the german emperor the king of spain and the king of france fight they private feud they bloody battle on she much coveted soil and by they destructive influence keep down all progress and foster every jealousy by the recollection of old the spirit of liberty be nowhere so dangerous for european absolutism as in italy and this spirit of republican liberty this warlike genius of ancient rome be never extinguish between the alp and the faro we be teach by the scribe of absolutism to speak of the italian as if they be a nation of coward and we forget that the most renowned master of the science of war the greatest general up to we day be italian -- piccolominus montecucculi farnese eugene of savoy spinolum and bonaparte -- a galaxy of name whose glory be dim only by the reflection that none of they fight for he own country as often as the spirit of liberty awake in italy the servile force of germany of spain and of france pour into the country and extinguish the glowing spark in the blood of the people lest it should once more illumine the dark night of europe frederic barbarossa destroy milan to its foundation when it minister of justice in hungary in answer to _ count casimir bathyanyus so early as the commencement of the serbian insurrection the popular suspicion gain ground that the insurrection have be stir up by the secret intrigue of the court and confidence in the truth and good faith of the king disappear accordingly the nation however still indulge the hope that a weak king though betray into ambiguous proceeding would not permit himself to be carry away into a flagrant breach of the constitution this be the time when the king in the opinion of the people be keep distinct from the camarillum but when the austrian ministry openly attempt to deprive hungary of its ministry of war and finance when the base game of the degradation and restoration of jellachich be play and when the hungarian army fighting in the name of the king against the insurrection of the serbian and croat become aware that the ball of that same king thin they rank from the hostile camp the nation arrive at the universal conviction that the hapsburg dynasty be only pursue they old absolute tendency and that they want to force hungary into self-defence in order under the pretext of rebellion to deprive it of all its constitutional rights and guarantee it need no proof that a loud indignation and even hatred of the dynasty spread far and wide in the country in consequence of these intrigue and proceedings in spite of this natural excitement and of the war itself carry on by the nation with a increase enthusiasm of hatred of the house of austrium no party in the country urge a declaration of _ déchéance _ or forfeiture against the dynasty even all the faithless act record in the letter of count casimir bathyanyus and the cruelty commit in the name of that court in lower hungary and transylvanium do not turn the scale in this direction the pragmatic sanction be still consider as good in law and the many precedent of we history when the nation and its king go to war with each other and ultimately settle they dispute by solemn pact confirm the constitution of the land convey the notion that a reconciliation be even then not impossible without these precedent and reminiscence of history and only guide by the universal feeling of the country against the dynasty the hungarian parliament would have pronounce the forfeiture of the house of austrium so far back as October 1848 when jellachich be appoint absolute plenipotentiary of the king in hungary with discretionary power of life and death or in December 1848 when in olmütz the succession of the hungarian throne be change and determine without the concurrence of the nation through the diet to force the nation and its parliament to the last step in this momentous crisis the court itself break the dynastic tie this be do by the imposition of the constitution of the 4th of march 1849 by which the house of austrium itself annihilate the pragmatic sanction treat free and independent hungary with the arrogance of a conqueror the nation more irritated by this act than by any precede event see that the hour be come beyond which further to defer the dethronement of the dynasty would be alike incompatible with the law and the honor of hungary _ all the channel of public opinion the public press the popular meeting and even the head quarter of the army resound with emphatic declaration of the impossibility of reconciliation with the dynasty the garrison of komorn _ -- the most important fortress of the country -- _ petition the government for the declaration of forfeiture _ most assuredly no party maneuver be want in this universal excitement cause by the constitution of the 4th of march to carry a parliamentary resolution of forfeiture when the proposition of forfeiture be make on the 14th of April 1849 in the house of representative only eight member vote against it in a house never attend by less than from 220 to 240 member the house of magnate adopt this resolution without opposition the press of all shades of opinion though enjoy the most unlimited freedom also declare for the resolution of the diet it be moreover receive throughout the whole country with patriotic assent and determination if there be a party oppose to the forfeiture how come it that it do not hold it to be a duty to declare its opposition in the diet or through the press when the intelligence of the unfortunate battle of temeswar reach the governor kossuth who be then in the fortress of arad he immediately summon a council of the ministry to deliberate on measure of public safety still possible at this council in which all the minister take part it be resolve to invest görgei who stand alone at the head of a unconquered army with full power for negotiate a peace it be moreover resolve to dissolve the government which could not be carry on in any fixed place of safety under the exist circumstance we do not however insert in the instrument invest görgei with full power -lrb- and despatch to he immediately -rrb- the abdication of the government on the same day -- it be the 11th of August 1849 -- görgei declare in the presence of some of the minister who have assemble at csányi 's -lrb- who be one of they -rrb- that he could not accept the commission because the resignation of the government be not contain in it while he be sure that the enemy would enter into no negotiation with he so long as kossuth and he ministry be think to be behind he the minister who be present after a short deliberation consider it to be they duty not to stand in the way of the negotiation which have be resolve on as necessary accordingly send they resignation to the governor _ whom they request to resign as well _ the governor soon after send he abdication for countersignature by these member of the ministry and accordingly the government formally dissolve itself after have do so _ de facto _ in the previous council of minister i must mention the circumstance that _ in the governor 's instrument of abdication condition be proscribe to görgei which be not insert in the original instrument of authorization issue by the full council _ these condition be the preservation of the nationality and the autonomy of hungary four minister take part in this resignation of the governor as above state aulich csányi horvath and i two of the minister szemere and -lrb- casimir -rrb- bathyanyus be absent when the formal declaration of the abdication be discuss at csányi 's residence i have not mention among the minister we late colleague the finance minister dushek because he treachery which be afterwards bring to light exclude he from we rank from all these circumstance it will be manifest how unjust the reproach of count casimir bathyanyus be that no new cabinet council be hold it be notorious that görgei abuse the full power with which he be entrust instead of procure the preservation of hungary by a negotiation for peace by a ignominious treachery to he native country from that very moment the power confer on he by the above-mentioned instrument and the conditional abdication of the government consequently and legally revert to he who have invest he with it to deny this would be to recognize in the foreign rule which crush hungary in consequence of that treachery legitimate right and lawful power i however perfectly agree with the noble count that the nation once more restore to its constitutional existence and free from foreign yoke will have the unlimited right to dispose of all the affair of the country and consequently of the executive power to assert a contrary opinion would be a crime against the nation not over a liberated nation -lrb- which of course would have the right to choose whom it will -rrb- but over a nation crush by a usurp power the claim of kossuth as elect governor of hungary be i submit lawful republican principle have not be proclaim at kossuth 's dictation as the aim of we national exertion they be during we struggle the well-ascertained and deep-rooted sentiment of the country and kossuth could only faithfully represent the proclaimed will and feeling of the nation by inscribe they on he banner immediately after the declaration of independence all the manifestation of the national will be unanimous in the desire for a republic the ministry which be nominate by the governor as a consequence of that legislative act declare in both house of the diet that its effort would be direct to the establishment of a republic both house join in this declaration and in the government no opposition whatever be manifest against it one of the first act of the new government be to remove the crown from all national scutcheon and from the great seal of hungary the press in all its shades develop republican principle the new semi-official paper bear the name of _ the republic _ it be true that the government be only provisional for the war continue and the definite decision of this question depend on unforeseen circumstance we should have prefer almost any settlement to the necessity of a subjection to the austrian dynasty and at the price of emancipation from that detest power the nation would even have be prepare for the sake of aid to choose a king from another race but certainly if it have be the unaided victor in the struggle never monarchical government would have be for we the resort of expediency the government of we wish and principle be the republic i do not feel at all convince as the noble count assert that the institution and habit of hungary be incompatible with a democratic republic i find on the contrary trait in they which lead I to a opposite conclusion the aggregate character of the numerous nobility which resign its privilege in the diet of 1847-48 of its own accord and which be in its nature more a democratic than a aristocratic body because neither territorial wealth nor rank interfere with or disturb the equality of its rights -- the national antipathy to the system of a upper house which be consider as a foreign institution because it have be introduce under the austrian dynasty -- the immemorial custom of periodically elect all official and even the judge -- the detestation in which bureaucracy and all the instrument of centralization be hold in all age while the attachment to the municipal self-government be ineradicable -- the fact that in consequence of the law which have be sanction in April 1848 the county authority formerly only elect from the nobility be democratically reconstitute and exercise they function in this form till the catastrophe of világos without the slightest collision between the different class of society -- the peaceful election of the representative of the last diet conduct almost on the principle of universal suffrage -- all these fact unmistakeably prove that the germ of democracy lay in we institution and that these could receive a democratic development without any concussion those characteristic _ trait _ of we nation which have be so often misrepresent as sign of a aversion to a republic and which may be more properly call civic virtue as for example we respect for law we antipathy to untried political theory we attachment to traditional custom and we pride in the history of we country be no obstacle to but rather guarantee and even condition of a republic which be to be national and endure it would indeed be a unprecedented event in history if staunch royalism could be the characteristic of a country which like hungary have find in its king for three hundred year the inexorable foe of its liberty and which in that time for its defense have to wage six bloody war against the dynasty as to the criticism by the noble count of the personal character of kossuth i take leave to assert that a great majority of the hungarian nation do not share he opinion it be not my task to appear as a personal advocate and i wish therefore to advert only to one point of he attack which may seem to be base on fact the noble count assert that kossuth have attain to power _ by doubtful means _ i be amaze at this assertion know as i do that kossuth be propose by count loui bathyanyus and nominate by the king with the universal applause of the nation to the ministry of finance after the resignation of the first hungarian ministry he be freely and unanimously elect by the diet to the presidency of the committee of defense and after the declare forfeiture of the dynasty to the governorship of the country i know no more honorable means by which a man can be raise to power s vukovic late minister in hungary in answer to _ prince esterhazy i shall now proceed to give a succinct account of what take place from April 14 when the new act receive the royal sanction to December 1848 you may be assure that i shall conceal nothing that tend to change the relation between hungary and austria the prime minister be already nominate when jellachich be raise to the dignity of ban of croatium by a royal decree which the premier be not even ask to countersign the hungarian minister nevertheless for the sake of peace overlook this irregular proceeding by a decree date June 10 1848 the king make know to all whom it might concern that all the troops station within the kingdom of hungary whether hungarian or austrian be place under the order of the hungarian minister of war and that all the hungarian fortress be under the jurisdiction of the say minister yet at this very time officer of the imperial and royal army be take a active part in the rebellion of the serb and valach while general mayerhofer be enlist recruit in the principality of servium and send they to assist the rebel the people thus behold with astonishment civil war break out and see with still greater astonishment that imperial officer be fight on both side jellachich as a functionary of the hungarian crown refuse to obey the hungarian ministry and illegally summon a croatian diet to meet at agram on June 5 in consequence of these proceedings ferdinand v by a decree date June 10 1848 deprive he as a rebel of all he civil and military office and dignity but at the same time send he through he minister of war lator field officer artillery and ammunition the trouble increase daily the hungarian ministry request the archduke john to act we mediator he accept the office but do nothing the diet meet on July 2 the palatine as the representative of the sovereign in the speech from the throne say that as several district be in a state of open rebellion the principal object to which in the name of he majesty he should direct the attention of the diet be the finances and the defence of the country and that bill relate to these object would be bring in by the minister he then proceed as follow : -- he majesty have learn with painful feeling that although he only follow the dictate of he own gracious inclination when at the request of the faithful hungarian people he give he sovereign sanction to the law enact by the last diet -- law which the common weal accord to the exigency of the present age render imperatively necessary -- there be nevertheless a number of seditious agitator especially in the annexed territory and the hungarian district of the lower danube who by false report and terrorism have excite the different religious sect and race speak different language against each other and by mendaciously affirm that the above-mentioned law be not the free expression of he majesty 's royal will have stir up the people to offer a armed opposition to the execution of the law and to the legally constitute authority and moreover that some of these agitator have even proceed so far in they iniquitous course as to spread the report that this armed opposition have be make in the interest of the dynasty and with the knowledge and connivance of he majesty or of the member of he majesty 's royal house i therefore in order that all the inhabitant of the kingdom without distinction as to creed or language may have they mind set at rest hereby declare in conformity with the sovereign behest of he majesty we most gracious king and in he sovereign name and person that it be he majesty 's firm and steadfast determination to defend with all he royal power and authority the unity and integrity of he royal hungarian crown against every attack from without and every attempt at disruption and separation that may be make within the kingdom and at the same time inviolably to maintain the law which have receive the royal sanction and while he majesty will not suffer any one to curtail the liberty assure to all class by the law he majesty as well as all the member of he royal dynasty strongly condemn the audacity of those who venture to affirm that any illegal act whatsoever or any disrespect of the constitute authority can be reconcileable with he majesty 's sovereign will or at all compatible with the interest of the royal dynasty it thus clearly appear that the king acknowledge the validity and the inviolability of the act pass by the diet of 1847-8 three month after they have be sanction rely on the sincerity of the royal asseveration the diet humbly request that he majesty would be graciously pleased to render the country happy by he presence it be in fact the general wish that the king should come to hungary even the most radical journal loudly declare that if he come he would be receive with enthusiasm border on madness meanwhile the rebellion of the croat serb and valach be spread daily and that too _ in the name of the sovereign _ general colonel and other field officer of the imperial army be at the head of it without any one of they be summon by the king to answer for he conduct the eye of the too credulous native be now open and still more when the king refuse to sanction the act for the levying of troops and raise of fund for the suppression of the rebellion although the diet have be convene chiefly for this purpose i must here observe that at this period nothing whatever have occur that could serve as a pretext for the dynasty to support the rebellion the diet it be true would not consent that the troops that be to be levy should be draught into the old regiment but it be obviously impossible for the diet to consent to any such measure at a period when the rebel be everywhere lead by imperial officer when the austrian troops station in hungary although they have be place under the order of the hungarian ministry refuse to fight against those rebel and the commander of fortress to receive order from the hungarian war-office on the 8th of September a deputation from the hungarian diet earnestly entreat he majesty to sanction two act relate to the levying of troops and tax the king refuse but in he answer to the address of the deputation say i trust that no one will hereby suppose that i have the intention to set aside or infringe the exist law this i repeat be far from my intention on the contrary it be my firm and determine will to maintain in conformity with my coronation oath the law the integrity and the rights of the kingdom under my hungarian crown the king make this solemn declaration on the 8th of September and on the 9th of September jellachich cross the drave with 48000 man to wage war in the king 's name on the hungarian diet and ministry the king have moreover on _ the 4th of September _ affix he sign manual to a letter or royal mandate address to jellachich and revoke the decree by which he have be deprive of he civil and military office and dignity he majesty plenipotentiary commissary for the kingdom of hungary and invest with unlimited authority to act in the name of he majesty within the say kingdom hungary so far from commence the revolution be not recognize a decree that suspend the constitution and invest jellachich with the dictatorship will be find quite natural if not by you at least by every englishman who cherish constitutional freedom dissolve before the budget for the ensue year have be vote from this short but faithful account of what actually occur it clearly appear that the hungarian nation have not recourse to arm until the ban of croatium enter the hungarian territory with a austrian-croatian army it be also a undeniable fact that until the promulgation of the austrian charter in march 1849 -- by which with a stroke of the pen the independence of hungary be destroy its constitution abolish and its territory dismember -- the hungarian nation never demand anything else than the maintenance of the law and institution which its sovereign have sanction and swear to maintain inviolate it be however precisely for the purpose of destroy these law and institution that the dynasty begin the war this of course they do not venture to avow it be necessary to conceal the real motive of they perfidious conduct from the civilized world hence in they public proclamation they always allege some pretext or other -- all of they equally groundless at the commencement they say that it be only a insignificant faction they have to deal with but when they see that the whole nation be array in arm against they they declare it be for the suppression of demagogueism propagate by foreigner chiefly pole that they army have enter hungary and to give a color to this pretext they industriously spread the report that there be 20000 pole in the rank of the hungarian when however it become notorious that no more than 1000 pole be fight under we national standard the austrian dynasty appear as the _ soi-disant _ champion and judge of the various nationality or race this answer well enough until the system of centralization show too clearly that a attempt would be make to germanize these nationality when the dynasty again veer about and leave nationality in the lurch take up the peasantry we consequently find the austrian government assure the washington cabinet -lrb- in the note of July 4 1851 -rrb- that they have wage war on hungary in order to crush a turbulent aristocracy that preach democracy with they tongue while they whole life consist in the daily exercise over they fellow-man of arbitrary power in the most repugnant form this last pretext so ostentatiously put forth lose however even its plausibility when contrast with the policy of the dynasty in 1848 for it be a undoubted fact that although the reform effect in we _ political _ institution at that period be consent to by the dynasty without much hesitation it require the most energetic remonstrance on the part of the diet to obtain the royal sanction to the act for the liberation of the peasant from feudal bondage it be precisely to the fact of all class without distinction be equally aware of the cabal of the dynasty that may be ascribe the success of the hungarian insurrection it be not _ one _ man nor a party nor a conspiracy nor terrorism that awaken that spontaneous enthusiasm with which the people rush to arm kossuth may have be the rally cry but he be not the cause of the war for several month the people have witness the equivocal conduct of the dynasty have see that its word be belie by its deed have see that the rebel be everywhere lead by imperial officer and finally behold jellachich a high functionary of the hungarian crown invade the country at the head of a austro-croatian army it be then and not till then that the nation cry as with one voice -- _ the king be a traitor _ from that day begin the hungarian revolution on that day the monarchical feeling be extinguish what no one have think it possible to accomplish be accomplish by the dynasty itself \* \* \* \* \* appendix iii -- _ extract from a letter to the ` daily news ' in February 1852 by a _ hungarian exile _ in reply to a letter from _
